# Slides Service

Slides

This service allows scripts to create, access, and modify Google Slides
files. See also the [Google Slides documentation](https://developers.google.com/slides)
for more details on the underlying features of the Slides service.

## Classes

|                                                     Name                                                      |                                                                                                                                    Brief description                                                                                                                                    |
|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [AffineTransform](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform)                | A 3x3 matrix used to transform source coordinates (x1, y1) into destination coordinates (x2, y2) according to matrix multiplication: ```text [ x2 ]   [ scaleX shearX translateX ] [ x1 ] [ y2 ] = [ shearY scaleY translateY ] [ y1 ] [ 1  ]   [   0      0        1      ] [ 1  ] ``` |
| [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | A builder for [AffineTransform](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform) objects.                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [AlignmentPosition](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/alignment-position)            | The alignment position to apply.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [ArrowStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/arrow-style)                          | The kinds of start and end forms with which linear geometry can be rendered.                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| [AutoText](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/auto-text)                              | An element of text that is dynamically replaced with content that can change over time, such as a slide number.                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [AutoTextType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/auto-text-type)                     | The types of auto text.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [Autofit](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit)                                 | Describes the autofit settings of a shape.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| [AutofitType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit-type)                        | The autofit types.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border)                                   | Describes the border around an element.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [CellMergeState](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/cell-merge-state)                 | The table cell merge states.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| [Color](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color)                                     | An opaque color                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [ColorScheme](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme)                        | A color scheme defines a mapping from members of [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) to the actual colors used to render them.                                                                                                |
| [ConnectionSite](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/connection-site)                  | The connection site on a `Page``Element` that can connect to a [connector](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#isConnector()).                                                                                                                              |
| [ContentAlignment](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/content-alignment)              | The content alignments for a [Shape](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape) or [TableCell](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell).                                                                                           |
| [DashStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/dash-style)                            | The kinds of dashes with which linear geometry can be rendered.                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [Fill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/fill)                                       | Describes the page element's background                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [FillType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/fill-type)                              | The kinds of fill.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [Group](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/group)                                     | A collection of [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element)s joined as a single unit.                                                                                                                                                        |
| [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                                     | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing an image.                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [Layout](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/layout)                                   | A layout in a presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| [Line](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line)                                       | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing a line.                                                                                                                                                                           |
| [LineCategory](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-category)                      | The line category.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [LineFill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-fill)                              | Describes the fill of a line or outline                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [LineFillType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-fill-type)                     | The kinds of line fill.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [LineType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-type)                              | The line types.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)                                       | A hypertext link.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type)                              | The types of a [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link).                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [List](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list)                                       | A list in the text.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| [ListPreset](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-preset)                          | Preset patterns of glyphs for lists in text.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| [ListStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style)                            | The list styling for a range of text.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [Master](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/master)                                   | A master in a presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| [NotesMaster](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/notes-master)                        | A notes master in a presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [NotesPage](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/notes-page)                            | A notes page in a presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [Page](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page)                                       | A page in a presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| [PageBackground](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-background)                  | Describes the page's background                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [PageBackgroundType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-background-type)         | The kinds of page backgrounds.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element)                        | A visual element rendered on a page.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| [PageElementRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element-range)             | A collection of one or more [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) instances.                                                                                                                                                           |
| [PageElementType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element-type)               | The page element type.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| [PageRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-range)                            | A collection of one or more [Page](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page) instances.                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [PageType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-type)                              | The page types.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [Paragraph](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph)                             | A segment of text terminated by a newline character.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| [ParagraphAlignment](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-alignment)          | The types of text alignment for a paragraph.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)                  | The styles of text that apply to entire paragraphs.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| [PictureFill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/picture-fill)                        | A fill that renders an image that's stretched to the dimensions of its container.                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [PlaceholderType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/placeholder-type)                | The placeholder types.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| [Point](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/point)                                     | A point representing a location.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [PredefinedLayout](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/predefined-layout)              | Predefined layouts.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| [Presentation](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/presentation)                       | A presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [Selection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection)                             | The user's selection in the active presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [SelectionType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection-type)                    | Type of [Selection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection).                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| [Shape](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape)                                     | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing a generic shape that does not have a more specific classification.                                                                                                                |
| [ShapeType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape-type)                            | The shape types.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [SheetsChart](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/sheets-chart)                        | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing a linked chart embedded from Google Sheets.                                                                                                                                       |
| [SheetsChartEmbedType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/sheets-chart-embed-type)    | The Sheets chart's embed type.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide)                                     | A slide in a presentation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| [SlideLinkingMode](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide-linking-mode)             | The mode of links between slides.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [SlidePosition](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide-position)                    | The relative position of a [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide).                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [SlidesApp](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slides-app)                            | Creates and opens [Presentations](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/presentation) that can be edited.                                                                                                                                                          |
| [SolidFill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/solid-fill)                            | A solid color fill.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| [SpacingMode](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/spacing-mode)                        | The different modes for paragraph spacing.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| [SpeakerSpotlight](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight)              | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing a speaker spotlight.                                                                                                                                                              |
| [Table](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table)                                     | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing a table.                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [TableCell](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell)                            | A cell in a table.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [TableCellRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell-range)                 | A collection of one or more [TableCell](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell) instances.                                                                                                                                                               |
| [TableColumn](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-column)                        | A column in a table.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| [TableRow](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-row)                              | A row in a table.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [TextBaselineOffset](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-baseline-offset)         | The text vertical offset from its normal position.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [TextDirection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-direction)                    | The directions text can flow in.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)                            | A segment of the text contents of a [Shape](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape) or a [TableCell](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell).                                                                                  |
| [TextStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-style)                            | The style of text.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [ThemeColor](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color)                          | A color that refers to an entry in the page's [ColorScheme](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme).                                                                                                                                                   |
| [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type)                 | The name of an entry in the page's color scheme.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                                     | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing a video.                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [VideoSourceType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video-source-type)               | The video source types.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [WordArt](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/word-art)                                | A [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) representing word art.                                                                                                                                                                         |

## [AffineTransform](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform)

### Methods

|                                                     Method                                                     |                                                  Return type                                                  |                                                                  Brief description                                                                   |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [getScaleX()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#getScaleX())         | `Number`                                                                                                      | Gets the X coordinate scaling element.                                                                                                               |
| [getScaleY()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#getScaleY())         | `Number`                                                                                                      | Gets the Y coordinate scaling element.                                                                                                               |
| [getShearX()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#getShearX())         | `Number`                                                                                                      | Gets the X coordinate shearing element.                                                                                                              |
| [getShearY()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#getShearY())         | `Number`                                                                                                      | Gets the Y coordinate shearing element.                                                                                                              |
| [getTranslateX()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#getTranslateX()) | `Number`                                                                                                      | Gets the X coordinate translation element in points.                                                                                                 |
| [getTranslateY()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#getTranslateY()) | `Number`                                                                                                      | Gets the Y coordinate translation element in points.                                                                                                 |
| [toBuilder()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform#toBuilder())         | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Returns a new [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) based on this transform. |

## [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder)

### Methods

|                                                                 Method                                                                 |                                                  Return type                                                  |                                                                         Brief description                                                                          |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [build()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#build())                                 | [AffineTransform](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform)                | Creates an [AffineTransform](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform) object initialized with the elements set in the builder. |
| [setScaleX(scaleX)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#setScaleX(Number))             | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Sets the X coordinate scaling element and returns the builder.                                                                                                     |
| [setScaleY(scaleY)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#setScaleY(Number))             | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Sets the Y coordinate scaling element and returns the builder.                                                                                                     |
| [setShearX(shearX)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#setShearX(Number))             | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Sets the X coordinate shearing element and returns the builder.                                                                                                    |
| [setShearY(shearY)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#setShearY(Number))             | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Sets the Y coordinate shearing element and returns the builder.                                                                                                    |
| [setTranslateX(translateX)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#setTranslateX(Number)) | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Sets the X coordinate translation element in points, and returns the builder.                                                                                      |
| [setTranslateY(translateY)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder#setTranslateY(Number)) | [AffineTransformBuilder](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/affine-transform-builder) | Sets the Y coordinate translation element in points, and returns the builder.                                                                                      |

## [AlignmentPosition](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/alignment-position)

### Properties

|      Property       |  Type  |           Description           |
|---------------------|--------|---------------------------------|
| `CENTER`            | `Enum` | Align to the center.            |
| `HORIZONTAL_CENTER` | `Enum` | Align to the horizontal center. |
| `VERTICAL_CENTER`   | `Enum` | Align to the vertical center.   |

## [ArrowStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/arrow-style)

### Properties

|    Property     |  Type  |              Description              |
|-----------------|--------|---------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`   | `Enum` | An arrow style that is not supported. |
| `NONE`          | `Enum` | No arrow.                             |
| `STEALTH_ARROW` | `Enum` | Arrow with notched back.              |
| `FILL_ARROW`    | `Enum` | Filled arrow.                         |
| `FILL_CIRCLE`   | `Enum` | Filled circle.                        |
| `FILL_SQUARE`   | `Enum` | Filled square.                        |
| `FILL_DIAMOND`  | `Enum` | Filled diamond.                       |
| `OPEN_ARROW`    | `Enum` | Hollow arrow.                         |
| `OPEN_CIRCLE`   | `Enum` | Hollow circle.                        |
| `OPEN_SQUARE`   | `Enum` | Hollow square.                        |
| `OPEN_DIAMOND`  | `Enum` | Hollow diamond.                       |

## [Autofit](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit)

### Methods

|                                                          Method                                                           |                                      Return type                                       |                                                                                                Brief description                                                                                                |
|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [disableAutofit()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit#disableAutofit())                   | [Autofit](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit)          | Sets the [AutofitType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit-type) of a shape to [AutofitType.NONE](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit-type#NONE). |
| [getAutofitType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit#getAutofitType())                   | [AutofitType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit-type) | Gets the [AutofitType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit-type) of the shape.                                                                                                   |
| [getFontScale()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit#getFontScale())                       | `Number`                                                                               | Gets the font scale applied to the shape.                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [getLineSpacingReduction()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit#getLineSpacingReduction()) | `Number`                                                                               | Gets the line spacing reduction applied to the shape.                                                                                                                                                           |

## [AutofitType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/autofit-type)

### Properties

|    Property     |  Type  |              Description               |
|-----------------|--------|----------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`   | `Enum` | An autofit type that is not supported. |
| `NONE`          | `Enum` | Autofit isn't applied.                 |
| `TEXT_AUTOFIT`  | `Enum` | Shrinks the text on overflow.          |
| `SHAPE_AUTOFIT` | `Enum` | Resizes the shape to fit the text.     |

## [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border)

|                                                      Method                                                      |                                    Return type                                     |                                             Brief description                                              |

| [getWeight()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border#getWeight())                     | `Number`                                                                           | Gets the thickness of the border in points.                                                                |
| [isVisible()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border#isVisible())                     | `Boolean`                                                                          | Gets whether the border is visible or not.                                                                 |
| [setDashStyle(style)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border#setDashStyle(DashStyle)) | [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border)        | Sets the [DashStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/dash-style) of the border. |
| [setTransparent()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border#setTransparent())           | [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border)        | Sets the border to be transparent.                                                                         |
| [setWeight(points)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border#setWeight(Number))         | [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border)        | Sets the thickness of the border in points.                                                                |

## [Color](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color)

### Methods

|                                              Method                                               |                                     Return type                                      |                                               Brief description                                                |
|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [asRgbColor()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color#asRgbColor())     | [RgbColor](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/base/rgb-color.html)            | Converts this color to an [RgbColor](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/base/rgb-color.html).           |
| [asThemeColor()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color#asThemeColor()) | [ThemeColor](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color) | Converts this color to a [ThemeColor](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color). |
| [getColorType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color#getColorType()) | [ColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/base/color-type.html)          | Get the type of this color.                                                                                    |

## [ColorScheme](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme)

### Methods

|                                                                                    Method                                                                                    |                                           Return type                                           |                                                                                                           Brief description                                                                                                            |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [getConcreteColor(theme)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme#getConcreteColor(ThemeColorType))                                          | [Color](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color)                       | Returns the concrete [Color](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color) associated with the [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) in this color scheme. |
| [getThemeColors()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme#getThemeColors())                                                                 | [ThemeColorType[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) | Returns a list of all possible theme color types in a color scheme.                                                                                                                                                                    |
| [setConcreteColor(type, color)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme#setConcreteColor(ThemeColorType,Color))                              | [ColorScheme](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme)          | Sets the concrete color associated with the [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) in this color scheme to the given color.                                                     |
| [setConcreteColor(type, red, green, blue)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme#setConcreteColor(ThemeColorType,Integer,Integer,Integer)) | [ColorScheme](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme)          | Sets the concrete color associated with the [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) in this color scheme to the given color in RGB format.                                       |
| [setConcreteColor(type, hexColor)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme#setConcreteColor(ThemeColorType,String))                          | [ColorScheme](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/color-scheme)          | Sets the concrete color associated with the [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) in this color scheme to the given color in HEX format.                                       |

## [ContentAlignment](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/content-alignment)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                       Description                       |
|---------------|--------|---------------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A content alignment that is not supported.              |
| `TOP`         | `Enum` | Aligns the content to the top of the content holder.    |
| `MIDDLE`      | `Enum` | Aligns the content to the middle of the content holder. |
| `BOTTOM`      | `Enum` | Aligns the content to the bottom of the content holder. |

## [DashStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/dash-style)

### Properties

|    Property     |  Type  |             Description             |
|-----------------|--------|-------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`   | `Enum` | A dash style that is not supported. |
| `SOLID`         | `Enum` | Solid line.                         |
| `DOT`           | `Enum` | Dotted line.                        |
| `DASH`          | `Enum` | Dashed line.                        |
| `DASH_DOT`      | `Enum` | Alternating dashes and dots.        |
| `LONG_DASH`     | `Enum` | Line with large dashes.             |
| `LONG_DASH_DOT` | `Enum` | Alternating large dashes and dots.  |

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                Description                 |
|---------------|--------|--------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A fill type that is not supported.         |
| `NONE`        | `Enum` | No fill, so the background is transparent. |
| `SOLID`       | `Enum` | A solid color fill.                        |

| [remove()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#remove())                                                           | `void`                                                                                          | Removes the page element.                                                                                                                                                                                       |

| [replace(blobSource)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#replace(BlobSource))                                     | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Replaces this image with an image described by a [`Blob``Source`](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/base/blob-source) object.                                                                 |
| [replace(blobSource, crop)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#replace(BlobSource,Boolean))                       | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Replaces this image with an image described by a [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image) object, optionally cropping the image to fit.                                        |
| [replace(imageUrl)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#replace(String))                                           | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Replaces this image with another image downloaded from the provided URL.                                                                                                                                        |
| [replace(imageUrl, crop)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#replace(String,Boolean))                             | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Replaces this image with another image downloaded from the provided URL, optionally cropping the image to fit.                                                                                                  |
| [scaleHeight(ratio)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#scaleHeight(Number))                                      | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Scales the element's height by the specified ratio.                                                                                                                                                             |
| [scaleWidth(ratio)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#scaleWidth(Number))                                        | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Scales the element's width by the specified ratio.                                                                                                                                                              |
| [select()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#select())                                                           | `void`                                                                                          | Selects only the [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) in the active presentation and removes any previous selection.                                          |
| [select(replace)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#select(Boolean))                                             | `void`                                                                                          | Selects the [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) in the active presentation.                                                                                  |
| [sendBackward()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#sendBackward())                                               | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sends the page element backward on the page by one element.                                                                                                                                                     |
| [sendToBack()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#sendToBack())                                                   | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sends the page element to the back of the page.                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [setDescription(description)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setDescription(String))                          | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the page element's alt text description.                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [setHeight(height)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setHeight(Number))                                         | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the element's height in points, which is the height of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                                                                        |
| [setLeft(left)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setLeft(Number))                                               | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the element's horizontal position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                                                             |
| [setLinkSlide(slideIndex)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setLinkSlide(Integer))                              | [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)                         | Sets a [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link) to the given [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide) using the zero-based index of the slide.  |
| [setLinkSlide(slide)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setLinkSlide(Slide))                                     | [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)                         | Sets a [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link) to the given [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide), the link is set by the given slide ID.   |
| [setLinkSlide(slidePosition)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setLinkSlide(SlidePosition))                     | [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)                         | Sets a [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link) to the given [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide) using the relative position of the slide. |
| [setLinkUrl(url)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setLinkUrl(String))                                          | [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)                         | Sets a [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link) to the given non-empty URL string.                                                                                               |
| [setRotation(angle)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setRotation(Number))                                      | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the element's clockwise rotation angle around its center in degrees.                                                                                                                                       |
| [setTitle(title)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setTitle(String))                                            | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the page element's alt text title.                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [setTop(top)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setTop(Number))                                                  | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the element's vertical position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                                                               |
| [setTransform(transform)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setTransform(AffineTransform))                       | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the transform of the page element with the provided transform.                                                                                                                                             |
| [setWidth(width)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image#setWidth(Number))                                            | [Image](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/image)                       | Sets the element's width in points, which is the width of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                                                                          |

## [Line](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line)

### Methods

|                                                                     Method                                                                     |                                           Return type                                           |                                                                                                Brief description                                                                                                |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [alignOnPage(alignmentPosition)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#alignOnPage(AlignmentPosition))               | [Line](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line)                         | Aligns the element to the specified alignment position on the page.                                                                                                                                             |
| [bringForward()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#bringForward())                                               | [Line](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line)                         | Brings the page element forward on the page by one element.                                                                                                                                                     |
| [bringToFront()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#bringToFront())                                               | [Line](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line)                         | Brings the page element to the front of the page.                                                                                                                                                               |
| [duplicate()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#duplicate())                                                     | [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element)          | Duplicates the page element.                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| [getConnectionSites()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getConnectionSites())                                   | [ConnectionSite[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/connection-site)  | Returns the list of `Connection``Site`s on the page element, or an empty list if the page element does not have any connection sites.                                                                           |
| [getDashStyle()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getDashStyle())                                               | [DashStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/dash-style)              | Gets the [DashStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/dash-style) of the line.                                                                                                        |
| [getDescription()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getDescription())                                           | `String`                                                                                        | Returns the page element's alt text description.                                                                                                                                                                |
| [getEnd()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getEnd())                                                           | [Point](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/point)                       | Returns the end point of the line, measured from the upper-left corner of the page.                                                                                                                             |
| [getEndArrow()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getEndArrow())                                                 | [ArrowStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/arrow-style)            | Gets the [ArrowStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/arrow-style) of the arrow at the end of the line.                                                                              |
| [getEndConnection()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getEndConnection())                                       | [ConnectionSite](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/connection-site)    | Returns the connection at the end of the line, or `null` if there is no connection.                                                                                                                             |
| [getHeight()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getHeight())                                                     | `Number`                                                                                        | Gets the element's height in points, which is the height of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                                                                        |
| [getInherentHeight()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getInherentHeight())                                     | `Number`                                                                                        | Returns the element's inherent height in points.                                                                                                                                                                |
| [getInherentWidth()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getInherentWidth())                                       | `Number`                                                                                        | Returns the element's inherent width in points.                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [getLeft()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getLeft())                                                         | `Number`                                                                                        | Returns the element's horizontal position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                                                          |
| [getLineCategory()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getLineCategory())                                         | [LineCategory](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-category)        | Gets the [LineCategory](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-category) of the line.                                                                                                  |
| [getLineFill()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getLineFill())                                                 | [LineFill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-fill)                | Gets the [LineFill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-fill) of the line.                                                                                                          |
| [getLineType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getLineType())                                                 | [LineType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-type)                | Gets the [LineType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-type) of the line.                                                                                                          |

| [getObjectId()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getObjectId())                                                 | `String`                                                                                        | Returns the unique ID for this object.                                                                                                                                                                          |

| [getParentGroup()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line#getParentGroup())                                           | [Group](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/group)                       | Returns the group this page element belongs to, or `null` if the element is not in a group.                                                                                                                     |

## [LineCategory](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-category)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                      Description                      |
|---------------|--------|-------------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A line category that is not supported.                |
| `STRAIGHT`    | `Enum` | Straight connectors, including straight connector 1.  |
| `BENT`        | `Enum` | Bent connectors, including bent connector 2 to 5.     |
| `CURVED`      | `Enum` | Curved connectors, including curved connector 2 to 5. |

## [LineFill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-fill)
