## [LineFillType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-fill-type)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                   Description                   |
|---------------|--------|-------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A line fill type that is not supported.         |
| `NONE`        | `Enum` | No fill, so the line or outline is transparent. |
| `SOLID`       | `Enum` | A solid color fill.                             |

## [LineType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/line-type)

### Properties

|        Property        |  Type  |            Description             |
|------------------------|--------|------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`          | `Enum` | A line type that is not supported. |
| `STRAIGHT_CONNECTOR_1` | `Enum` | Straight connector 1 form.         |
| `BENT_CONNECTOR_2`     | `Enum` | Bent connector 2 form.             |
| `BENT_CONNECTOR_3`     | `Enum` | Bent connector 3 form.             |
| `BENT_CONNECTOR_4`     | `Enum` | Bent connector 4 form.             |
| `BENT_CONNECTOR_5`     | `Enum` | Bent connector 5 form.             |
| `CURVED_CONNECTOR_2`   | `Enum` | Curved connector 2 form.           |
| `CURVED_CONNECTOR_3`   | `Enum` | Curved connector 3 form.           |
| `CURVED_CONNECTOR_4`   | `Enum` | Curved connector 4 form.           |
| `CURVED_CONNECTOR_5`   | `Enum` | Curved connector 5 form.           |
| `STRAIGHT_LINE`        | `Enum` | Straight line.                     |

## [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)

### Methods

|                                                  Method                                                  |                                        Return type                                         |                                                                                                                                                                                                    Brief description                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [getLinkType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link#getLinkType())           | [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type)           | Returns the [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| [getLinkedSlide()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link#getLinkedSlide())     | [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide)                  | Returns the linked [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide) for non-URL links types, if it exists.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| [getSlideId()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link#getSlideId())             | `String`                                                                                   | Returns the ID of the linked [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide) or `null` if the [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type) is not [LinkType.SLIDE_ID](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type#SLIDE_ID).                                                                                                     |
| [getSlideIndex()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link#getSlideIndex())       | `Integer`                                                                                  | Returns the zero-based index of the linked [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide) or `null` if the [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type) is not [LinkType.SLIDE_INDEX](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type#SLIDE_INDEX).                                                                                 |
| [getSlidePosition()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link#getSlidePosition()) | [SlidePosition](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide-position) | Returns the [SlidePosition](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide-position) of the linked [Slide](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide) or `null` if the [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type) is not [LinkType.SLIDE_POSITION](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type#SLIDE_POSITION). |
| [getUrl()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link#getUrl())                     | `String`                                                                                   | Returns the URL to the external web page or `null` if the [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type) is not [LinkType.URL](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type#URL).                                                                                                                                                                             |

## [LinkType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link-type)

### Properties

|     Property     |  Type  |                                     Description                                     |
|------------------|--------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`    | `Enum` | A link type that is not supported.                                                  |
| `URL`            | `Enum` | A link to an external web page.                                                     |
| `SLIDE_POSITION` | `Enum` | A link to a specific slide in this presentation, addressed by its position.         |
| `SLIDE_ID`       | `Enum` | A link to a specific slide in this presentation, addressed by its ID.               |
| `SLIDE_INDEX`    | `Enum` | A link to a specific slide in this presentation, addressed by its zero-based index. |

## [List](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list)

### Methods

|                                                   Method                                                   |                                     Return type                                     |                                                Brief description                                                |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [getListId()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list#getListId())                 | `String`                                                                            | Returns the ID of the list.                                                                                     |
| [getListParagraphs()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list#getListParagraphs()) | [Paragraph[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph) | Returns all the [Paragraphs](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph) in the list. |

## [ListPreset](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-preset)

### Properties

|            Property             |  Type  |                                                           Description                                                            |
|---------------------------------|--------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `DISC_CIRCLE_SQUARE`            | `Enum` | A list with a \`DISC\`, \`CIRCLE\` and \`SQUARE\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                                    |
| `DIAMONDX_ARROW3D_SQUARE`       | `Enum` | A list with a \`DIAMONDX\`, \`ARROW3D\` and \`SQUARE\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                               |
| `CHECKBOX`                      | `Enum` | A list with \`CHECKBOX\` glyphs for all list nesting levels.                                                                     |
| `ARROW_DIAMOND_DISC`            | `Enum` | A list with a \`ARROW\`, \`DIAMOND\` and \`DISC\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                                    |
| `STAR_CIRCLE_SQUARE`            | `Enum` | A list with a \`STAR\`, \`CIRCLE\` and \`SQUARE\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                                    |
| `ARROW3D_CIRCLE_SQUARE`         | `Enum` | A list with a \`ARROW3D\`, \`CIRCLE\` and \`SQUARE\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                                 |
| `LEFTTRIANGLE_DIAMOND_DISC`     | `Enum` | A list with a \`LEFTTRIANGLE\`, \`DIAMOND\` and \`DISC\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                             |
| `DIAMONDX_HOLLOWDIAMOND_SQUARE` | `Enum` | A list with a \`DIAMONDX\`, \`HOLLOWDIAMOND\` and \`SQUARE\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                         |
| `DIAMOND_CIRCLE_SQUARE`         | `Enum` | A list with a \`DIAMOND\`, \`CIRCLE\` and \`SQUARE\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels.                                 |
| `DIGIT_ALPHA_ROMAN`             | `Enum` | A list with \`DIGIT\`, \`ALPHA\` and \`ROMAN\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels, followed by periods.                  |
| `DIGIT_ALPHA_ROMAN_PARENS`      | `Enum` | A list with \`DIGIT\`, \`ALPHA\` and \`ROMAN\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels, followed by parenthesis.              |
| `DIGIT_NESTED`                  | `Enum` | A list with \`DIGIT\` glyphs separated by periods, where each nesting level uses the previous nesting level's glyph as a prefix. |
| `UPPERALPHA_ALPHA_ROMAN`        | `Enum` | A list with \`UPPERALPHA\`, \`ALPHA\` and \`ROMAN\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels, followed by periods.             |
| `UPPERROMAN_UPPERALPHA_DIGIT`   | `Enum` | A list with \`UPPERROMAN\`, \`UPPERALPHA\` and \`DIGIT\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels, followed by periods.        |
| `ZERODIGIT_ALPHA_ROMAN`         | `Enum` | A list with \`ZERODIGIT\`, \`ALPHA\` and \`ROMAN\` glyphs for the first 3 list nesting levels, followed by periods.              |

## [ListStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style)

### Methods

|                                                              Method                                                              |                                    Return type                                     |                                                                                                  Brief description                                                                                                  |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [applyListPreset(listPreset)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style#applyListPreset(ListPreset)) | [ListStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style) | Applies the specified [ListPreset](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-preset) to all of the paragraphs that overlap with the text.                                                     |
| [getGlyph()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style#getGlyph())                                   | `String`                                                                           | Returns the rendered glyph for the text.                                                                                                                                                                            |
| [getList()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style#getList())                                     | [List](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list)            | Returns the [List](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list) the text is in, or `null` if none of the text is in a list, or part of the text is in a list, or the text is in multiple lists. |
| [getNestingLevel()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style#getNestingLevel())                     | `Integer`                                                                          | Returns the 0-based nesting level of the text.                                                                                                                                                                      |
| [isInList()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style#isInList())                                   | `Boolean`                                                                          | Returns `true` if the text is in exactly one list, `false` if none of the text is in a list, and `null` if only some of the text is in a list or if the text is in multiple lists.                                  |
| [removeFromList()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style#removeFromList())                       | [ListStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style) | Removes the paragraphs that overlap with the text from any lists.                                                                                                                                                   |

| [replaceAllText(findText, replaceText, matchCase)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page#replaceAllText(String,String,Boolean))                                              | `Integer`                                                                                    | Replaces all instances of text matching find text with replace text.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [selectAsCurrentPage()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page#selectAsCurrentPage())                                                                                         | `void`                                                                                       | Selects the [Page](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page) in the active presentation as the [current page selection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection#getCurrentPage()) and removes any previous selection.                                  |

## [PageBackgroundType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-background-type)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                  Description                  |
|---------------|--------|-----------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A page background type that is not supported. |
| `NONE`        | `Enum` | No fill, so the background is rendered white. |
| `SOLID`       | `Enum` | A solid color fill.                           |
| `PICTURE`     | `Enum` | A picture that is stretched to fill the page. |

## [PageElementType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element-type)

### Properties

|      Property       |  Type  |                                    Description                                    |
|---------------------|--------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`       | `Enum` | Represents a page element that is not supported and cannot be further classified. |
| `SHAPE`             | `Enum` | Represents a generic shape that does not have a more specific classification.     |
| `IMAGE`             | `Enum` | Represents an image.                                                              |
| `VIDEO`             | `Enum` | Represents a video.                                                               |
| `TABLE`             | `Enum` | Represents a table.                                                               |
| `GROUP`             | `Enum` | Represents a collection of page elements joined as a single unit.                 |
| `LINE`              | `Enum` | Represents a line.                                                                |
| `WORD_ART`          | `Enum` | Represents word art.                                                              |
| `SHEETS_CHART`      | `Enum` | Represents a linked chart embedded from Google Sheets.                            |
| `SPEAKER_SPOTLIGHT` | `Enum` | Represents a speaker spotlight.                                                   |

| [setIndentFirstLine(indent)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setIndentFirstLine(Number))                      | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the indentation for the first line of paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) in points.                                                                                                                                    |
| [setIndentStart(indent)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setIndentStart(Number))                              | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the text start indentation for paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) in points.                                                                                                                                           |
| [setLineSpacing(spacing)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setLineSpacing(Number))                             | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the line spacing.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [setParagraphAlignment(alignment)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setParagraphAlignment(ParagraphAlignment)) | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the [ParagraphAlignment](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-alignment) of paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range).                                                                        |
| [setSpaceAbove(space)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setSpaceAbove(Number))                                 | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the extra space above paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) in points.                                                                                                                                                    |
| [setSpaceBelow(space)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setSpaceBelow(Number))                                 | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the extra space below paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) in points.                                                                                                                                                    |
| [setSpacingMode(mode)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setSpacingMode(SpacingMode))                           | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the [SpacingMode](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/spacing-mode) for paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range).                                                                                     |
| [setTextDirection(direction)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style#setTextDirection(TextDirection))                | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style)         | Sets the [TextDirection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-direction) for paragraphs in the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range).                                                                                 |

| `BODY`           | `Enum` | Body text.                                |
| `CHART`          | `Enum` | Chart or graph.                           |
| `CLIP_ART`       | `Enum` | Clip art image.                           |
| `CENTERED_TITLE` | `Enum` | Title centered.                           |
| `DIAGRAM`        | `Enum` | Diagram.                                  |
| `DATE_AND_TIME`  | `Enum` | Date and time.                            |
| `FOOTER`         | `Enum` | Footer text.                              |
| `HEADER`         | `Enum` | Header text.                              |
| `MEDIA`          | `Enum` | Multimedia.                               |
| `OBJECT`         | `Enum` | Any content type.                         |
| `PICTURE`        | `Enum` | Picture.                                  |
| `SLIDE_NUMBER`   | `Enum` | Number of a slide.                        |
| `SUBTITLE`       | `Enum` | Subtitle.                                 |
| `TABLE`          | `Enum` | Table.                                    |
| `TITLE`          | `Enum` | Slide title.                              |
| `SLIDE_IMAGE`    | `Enum` | Slide image.                              |

## [PredefinedLayout](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/predefined-layout)

### Properties

|            Property             |  Type  |                                Description                                 |
|---------------------------------|--------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`                   | `Enum` | A layout that is not supported.                                            |
| `BLANK`                         | `Enum` | Blank layout, with no placeholders.                                        |
| `CAPTION_ONLY`                  | `Enum` | Layout with a caption at the bottom.                                       |
| `TITLE`                         | `Enum` | Layout with a title and a subtitle.                                        |
| `TITLE_AND_BODY`                | `Enum` | Layout with a title and body.                                              |
| `TITLE_AND_TWO_COLUMNS`         | `Enum` | Layout with a title and two columns.                                       |
| `TITLE_ONLY`                    | `Enum` | Layout with only a title.                                                  |
| `SECTION_HEADER`                | `Enum` | Layout with a section title.                                               |
| `SECTION_TITLE_AND_DESCRIPTION` | `Enum` | Layout with a title and subtitle on one side and description on the other. |
| `ONE_COLUMN_TEXT`               | `Enum` | Layout with one title and one body, arranged in a single column.           |
| `MAIN_POINT`                    | `Enum` | Layout with a main point.                                                  |
| `BIG_NUMBER`                    | `Enum` | Layout with a big number heading.                                          |

## [Selection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection)

### Methods

|                                                       Method                                                        |                                            Return type                                            |                                                                                                                                                                                  Brief description                                                                                                                                                                                  |

| [getPageElementRange()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection#getPageElementRange()) | [PageElementRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element-range) | Returns the [PageElementRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element-range) collection of [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) instances that are selected or `null` if there are no [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) instances selected. |
| [getPageRange()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection#getPageRange())               | [PageRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-range)                | Returns the [PageRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-range) a collection of [Page](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page) instances in the flimstrip that are selected or `null` if the selection is not of type [SelectionType.PAGE](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection-type#PAGE). |
| [getSelectionType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection#getSelectionType())       | [SelectionType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection-type)        | Returns the [SelectionType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection-type).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| [getTableCellRange()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection#getTableCellRange())     | [TableCellRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell-range)     | Returns the [TableCellRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell-range) collection of [TableCell](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell) instances that are selected or `null` if there are no [TableCell](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/table-cell) instances selected.             |
| [getTextRange()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection#getTextRange())               | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)                | Returns the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) that is selected or `null` if the selection is not of type [SelectionType.TEXT](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection-type#TEXT).                                                                                                                     |

## [SelectionType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/selection-type)

### Properties

|    Property    |  Type  |                Description                 |
|----------------|--------|--------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`  | `Enum` | A selection type that is not supported.    |
| `NONE`         | `Enum` | No selection.                              |
| `TEXT`         | `Enum` | Text selection.                            |
| `TABLE_CELL`   | `Enum` | Table cell selection.                      |
| `PAGE`         | `Enum` | Page selection in the thumbnail flimstrip. |
| `PAGE_ELEMENT` | `Enum` | Page element selection.                    |
| `CURRENT_PAGE` | `Enum` | Current page selection.                    |

| [getBorder()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getBorder())                                                                 | [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border)                      | Returns the [Border](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/border) of the shape.                                                                                                           |
| [getConnectionSites()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getConnectionSites())                                               | [ConnectionSite[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/connection-site)   | Returns the list of `Connection``Site`s on the page element, or an empty list if the page element does not have any connection sites.                                                                           |
| [getContentAlignment()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getContentAlignment())                                             | [ContentAlignment](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/content-alignment) | Returns the [ContentAlignment](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/content-alignment) of the text in the shape.                                                                          |
| [getDescription()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getDescription())                                                       | `String`                                                                                         | Returns the page element's alt text description.                                                                                                                                                                |
| [getFill()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getFill())                                                                     | [Fill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/fill)                          | Returns the [Fill](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/fill) of the shape.                                                                                                               |
| [getHeight()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getHeight())                                                                 | `Number`                                                                                         | Gets the element's height in points, which is the height of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                                                                        |
| [getInherentHeight()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getInherentHeight())                                                 | `Number`                                                                                         | Returns the element's inherent height in points.                                                                                                                                                                |
| [getInherentWidth()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getInherentWidth())                                                   | `Number`                                                                                         | Returns the element's inherent width in points.                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [getLeft()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getLeft())                                                                     | `Number`                                                                                         | Returns the element's horizontal position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                                                          |
| [getLink()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getLink())                                                                     | [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)                          | Returns the [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link) or `null` if there is no link.                                                                                              |
| [getObjectId()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getObjectId())                                                             | `String`                                                                                         | Returns the unique ID for this object.                                                                                                                                                                          |

| [getParentGroup()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getParentGroup())                                                       | [Group](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/group)                        | Returns the group this page element belongs to, or `null` if the element is not in a group.                                                                                                                     |
| [getParentPage()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getParentPage())                                                         | [Page](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page)                          | Returns the page this page element is on.                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [getParentPlaceholder()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getParentPlaceholder())                                           | [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element)           | Returns the parent page element of the placeholder.                                                                                                                                                             |

| [getRotation()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/shape#getRotation())                                                             | `Number`                                                                                         | Returns the element's clockwise rotation angle around its center in degrees, where zero degrees means no rotation.                                                                                              |

## [SheetsChart](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/sheets-chart)

### Methods

|                                                                         Method                                                                         |                                                Return type                                                 |                                                                                                Brief description                                                                                                |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|

## [SheetsChartEmbedType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/sheets-chart-embed-type)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                                Description                                 |
|---------------|--------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | Represents a chart that is not supported and cannot be further classified. |
| `IMAGE`       | `Enum` | Indicates that the chart is embedded as an image.                          |

## [SlideLinkingMode](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide-linking-mode)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                Description                 |
|---------------|--------|--------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A slide linking mode that isn't supported. |
| `LINKED`      | `Enum` | Indicates that slides are linked.          |
| `NOT_LINKED`  | `Enum` | Indicates that slides aren't linked.       |

## [SlidePosition](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/slide-position)

### Properties

|     Property     |  Type  |             Description              |
|------------------|--------|--------------------------------------|
| `NEXT_SLIDE`     | `Enum` | The next slide.                      |
| `PREVIOUS_SLIDE` | `Enum` | The previous slide.                  |
| `FIRST_SLIDE`    | `Enum` | The first slide in the presentation. |
| `LAST_SLIDE`     | `Enum` | The last slide in the presentation.  |

## [SpacingMode](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/spacing-mode)

### Properties

|     Property     |  Type  |                     Description                     |
|------------------|--------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`    | `Enum` | A spacing mode that is not supported.               |
| `NEVER_COLLAPSE` | `Enum` | Paragraph spacing is always rendered.               |
| `COLLAPSE_LISTS` | `Enum` | Paragraph spacing is skipped between list elements. |

| [sendToBack()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight#sendToBack())                                                   | [SpeakerSpotlight](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight) | Sends the page element to the back of the page.                                                                                                                             |
| [setDescription(description)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight#setDescription(String))                          | [SpeakerSpotlight](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight) | Sets the page element's alt text description.                                                                                                                               |
| [setHeight(height)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight#setHeight(Number))                                         | [SpeakerSpotlight](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight) | Sets the element's height in points, which is the height of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                                    |
| [setLeft(left)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight#setLeft(Number))                                               | [SpeakerSpotlight](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight) | Sets the element's horizontal position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                         |

| [setTitle(title)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight#setTitle(String))                                            | [SpeakerSpotlight](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/speaker-spotlight) | Sets the page element's alt text title.                                                                                                                                     |

## [TextBaselineOffset](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-baseline-offset)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                  Description                   |
|---------------|--------|------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | An text baseline offset that is not supported. |
| `NONE`        | `Enum` | The text is not vertically offset.             |
| `SUPERSCRIPT` | `Enum` | The text is vertically offset upwards.         |
| `SUBSCRIPT`   | `Enum` | The text is vertically offset downwards.       |

## [TextDirection](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-direction)

### Properties

|    Property     |  Type  |               Description               |
|-----------------|--------|-----------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`   | `Enum` | A text direction that is not supported. |
| `LEFT_TO_RIGHT` | `Enum` | The text goes from left to right.       |
| `RIGHT_TO_LEFT` | `Enum` | The text goes from right to left.       |

## [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)

### Methods

|                                                                                   Method                                                                                   |                                         Return type                                          |                                                                                            Brief description                                                                                             |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| [appendParagraph(text)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#appendParagraph(String))                                                     | [Paragraph](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph)            | Appends a paragraph at the end of the text range.                                                                                                                                                        |
| [appendRange(textRange)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#appendRange(TextRange))                                                     | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Appends a copy of the provided text range to the end of the current text range.                                                                                                                          |
| [appendRange(textRange, matchSourceFormatting)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#appendRange(TextRange,Boolean))                      | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Appends a copy of the provided text range to the end of the current text range.                                                                                                                          |
| [appendText(text)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#appendText(String))                                                               | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Appends text at the end of the text range.                                                                                                                                                               |
| [asRenderedString()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#asRenderedString())                                                             | `String`                                                                                     | Returns the rendered text bounded by this range of the associated shape or table cell in a format appropriate to display to end users.                                                                   |
| [asString()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#asString())                                                                             | `String`                                                                                     | Returns the raw text bounded by this range of the associated shape or table cell.                                                                                                                        |
| [clear()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#clear())                                                                                   | `void`                                                                                       | Clears the text bounded by this range.                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [clear(startOffset, endOffset)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#clear(Integer,Integer))                                              | `void`                                                                                       | Clears the text bounded by the start and end offsets in the range.                                                                                                                                       |
| [find(pattern)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#find(String))                                                                        | [TextRange[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)         | Returns all the ranges matching the search pattern in the current text range.                                                                                                                            |
| [find(pattern, startOffset)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#find(String,Integer))                                                   | [TextRange[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)         | Returns all the ranges matching the search pattern in the current text range starting from the start offset.                                                                                             |
| [getAutoTexts()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getAutoTexts())                                                                     | [AutoText[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/auto-text)           | Returns the auto texts within the current text range.                                                                                                                                                    |
| [getEndIndex()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getEndIndex())                                                                       | `Integer`                                                                                    | Returns the exclusive, 0-based index for the last character in this range.                                                                                                                               |
| [getLength()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getLength())                                                                           | `Integer`                                                                                    | Returns the number of characters in this range.                                                                                                                                                          |
| [getLinks()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getLinks())                                                                             | [TextRange[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)         | Returns a collection of text ranges that correspond to all [Link](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/link)s within the current text range or overlapping the current text range. |
| [getListParagraphs()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getListParagraphs())                                                           | [Paragraph[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph)          | Returns the paragraphs in lists that overlap the current text range.                                                                                                                                     |
| [getListStyle()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getListStyle())                                                                     | [ListStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style)           | Returns the [ListStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/list-style) of the current text range.                                                                                |
| [getParagraphStyle()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getParagraphStyle())                                                           | [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style) | Returns the [ParagraphStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph-style) of the current text range.                                                                      |
| [getParagraphs()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getParagraphs())                                                                   | [Paragraph[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph)          | Returns the paragraphs that overlap the current text range.                                                                                                                                              |
| [getRange(startOffset, endOffset)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getRange(Integer,Integer))                                        | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Returns a new [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) covering part of the range from which it is derived.                                                    |
| [getRuns()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getRuns())                                                                               | [TextRange[]](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)         | Returns the text runs that overlap the current text range.                                                                                                                                               |
| [getStartIndex()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getStartIndex())                                                                   | `Integer`                                                                                    | Returns the inclusive, 0-based index for the first character in this range.                                                                                                                              |
| [getTextStyle()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#getTextStyle())                                                                     | [TextStyle](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-style)           | Returns the text style of the range, or `null` if the range is empty.                                                                                                                                    |
| [insertParagraph(startOffset, text)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#insertParagraph(Integer,String))                                | [Paragraph](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/paragraph)            | Inserts a paragraph at the start offset.                                                                                                                                                                 |
| [insertRange(startOffset, textRange)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#insertRange(Integer,TextRange))                                | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Inserts a copy of the provided text range at the start offset.                                                                                                                                           |
| [insertRange(startOffset, textRange, matchSourceFormatting)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#insertRange(Integer,TextRange,Boolean)) | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Inserts a copy of the provided text range at the start offset.                                                                                                                                           |
| [insertText(startOffset, text)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#insertText(Integer,String))                                          | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Inserts text at the start offset.                                                                                                                                                                        |
| [isEmpty()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#isEmpty())                                                                               | `Boolean`                                                                                    | Returns `true` if there are no characters in this range, and returns `false` otherwise.                                                                                                                  |
| [replaceAllText(findText, replaceText)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#replaceAllText(String,String))                               | `Integer`                                                                                    | Replaces all instances of text matching find text with replace text.                                                                                                                                     |
| [replaceAllText(findText, replaceText, matchCase)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#replaceAllText(String,String,Boolean))            | `Integer`                                                                                    | Replaces all instances of text matching find text with replace text.                                                                                                                                     |
| [select()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#select())                                                                                 | `void`                                                                                       | Selects only the [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range) in the active presentation and removes any previous selection.                                       |
| [setText(newText)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range#setText(String))                                                                  | [TextRange](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/text-range)           | Sets the text bounded by this range of the associated shape or table cell.                                                                                                                               |

## [ThemeColor](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color)

### Methods

|                                                      Method                                                       |                                          Return type                                          |            Brief description            |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------|
| [getColorType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color#getColorType())           | [ColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/base/color-type.html)                   | Get the type of this color.             |
| [getThemeColorType()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color#getThemeColorType()) | [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type) | Get the theme color type of this color. |

## [ThemeColorType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/theme-color-type)

### Properties

|       Property       |  Type  |                     Description                     |
|----------------------|--------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED`        | `Enum` | Represents a theme color that is not supported.     |
| `DARK1`              | `Enum` | Represents the first dark color.                    |
| `LIGHT1`             | `Enum` | Represents the first light color.                   |
| `DARK2`              | `Enum` | Represents the second dark color.                   |
| `LIGHT2`             | `Enum` | Represents the second light color.                  |
| `ACCENT1`            | `Enum` | Represents the first accent color.                  |
| `ACCENT2`            | `Enum` | Represents the second accent color.                 |
| `ACCENT3`            | `Enum` | Represents the third accent color.                  |
| `ACCENT4`            | `Enum` | Represents the fourth accent color.                 |
| `ACCENT5`            | `Enum` | Represents the fifth accent color.                  |
| `ACCENT6`            | `Enum` | Represents the sixth accent color.                  |
| `HYPERLINK`          | `Enum` | Represents the color to use for hyperlinks.         |
| `FOLLOWED_HYPERLINK` | `Enum` | Represents the color to use for visited hyperlinks. |

| [scaleWidth(ratio)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#scaleWidth(Number))                                        | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Scales the element's width by the specified ratio.                                                                                                                     |
| [select()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#select())                                                           | `void`                                                                                          | Selects only the [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) in the active presentation and removes any previous selection. |
| [select(replace)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#select(Boolean))                                             | `void`                                                                                          | Selects the [PageElement](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/page-element) in the active presentation.                                         |
| [sendBackward()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#sendBackward())                                               | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sends the page element backward on the page by one element.                                                                                                            |
| [sendToBack()](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#sendToBack())                                                   | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sends the page element to the back of the page.                                                                                                                        |
| [setDescription(description)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setDescription(String))                          | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the page element's alt text description.                                                                                                                          |
| [setHeight(height)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setHeight(Number))                                         | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the element's height in points, which is the height of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                               |
| [setLeft(left)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setLeft(Number))                                               | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the element's horizontal position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                    |
| [setRotation(angle)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setRotation(Number))                                      | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the element's clockwise rotation angle around its center in degrees.                                                                                              |
| [setTitle(title)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setTitle(String))                                            | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the page element's alt text title.                                                                                                                                |
| [setTop(top)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setTop(Number))                                                  | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the element's vertical position in points, measured from the upper-left corner of the page when the element has no rotation.                                      |
| [setTransform(transform)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setTransform(AffineTransform))                       | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the transform of the page element with the provided transform.                                                                                                    |
| [setWidth(width)](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video#setWidth(Number))                                            | [Video](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video)                       | Sets the element's width in points, which is the width of the element's bounding box when the element has no rotation.                                                 |

## [VideoSourceType](https://developers.google.com/apps-script/reference/slides/video-source-type)

### Properties

|   Property    |  Type  |                Description                 |
|---------------|--------|--------------------------------------------|
| `UNSUPPORTED` | `Enum` | A video source type that is not supported. |
| `YOUTUBE`     | `Enum` | YouTube video.                             |
